Now, several visits later, it's the only thing I've had there.  It's that good.  Definitely get the pickles, they're the best I've ever had.  And the butterscotch pudding.  I wouldn't have ordered it, but our server kind of made me, and I'm glad she did.  I tell anyone I know going to Vegas to go get a burger at BO.
